           The `move_base` actions require a `btraj` as the third parameter. When a `move_base` action is listed without a named `btraj` (e.g., `(move_base #o3 #q0 #o0)`), it means `#o0` is a `btraj`. So my previous plan used the correct `btraj` values (the `#t` values were `btraj`s that only occurred in `kin` actions, not `move_base`). The error was in using `t5` and `t6` which are specifically `btraj` objects used in other `kin` facts, but not valid `btraj` parameters for direct `move_base` calls between arbitrary base configurations. I should have used `#o0` which is provided as a general `btraj` for base movements between many `q` values.
